  if r < 0 || h < 0 then 0
  else if r = 0 && h = 0 then 1

 (* Write a function to find the volume of a cone. *)
let rec vol_cone r h =
  if r < 0 || h < 0 then 0
  else if r = 0 && h = 0 then 1
  else if r = 0 && h > 0 then 2
  else if r > 0 && h = 0 then 3
